LGBRC Sunday Road Ride

Hello team, This Sunday's road ride will head towards Steven's Canyon in the counter clockwise direction. We will regroup for bathroom/water at the intersection of Steven's Canyon and Mt. Eden before heading up Mt. Eden and regrouping again at the top of Pierce. Then, we'll climb Hwy 9 to the intersection of Redwood Gulch before heading back down Hwy 9 and back to the shop. Wheels roll at 8:35am.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] Saturday Road Ride on December 7th

Dear Fellow teammates, We have again a great forecast for this weekend apart from some colder temperatures. The plan for this Saturday is to paceline all together on a flatter route and head North. As always, we will stop and regroup to make sure the peloton stays together and we do not miss any important turns. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

78VP6T 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes üå• 57f ‚ûú üå§ 79f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òïÔ∏è Brew Story (22.43M) 16889 Beach Blvd, Huntington Beach, CA 92647 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Sunday Ride

Hello team, There is a good probability that we will have rain this Sunday. If the forecast shows rain for Sunday morning, this ride will be canceled. In the event that we have dry or dry-ish conditions this Sunday, we will meet at MBLG to head south to climb and descend IBM from the same direction. Before climbing IBM, we will stop for bathroom and water at the top of Mockingbird. Wheels roll at 8:35am sharp.

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Sunday Ride

Hi team, Presuming that we don't have rain this week, let's head up Redwood Gulch on Sunday. The road is gorgeous this year with the changing color of the leaves. Wheels roll at 8:35am. Route is subject to change depending on weather and road conditions.

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes üå• 52f ‚ûú üå§ 76f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 ‚òïÔ∏è Oslo Coffee Co (21.23M) 25642 Crown Valley Pkwy Suite E1, Ladera Ranch, CA 92694 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÄ 53f ‚ûú ‚òÄ 72f Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: üÖøÔ∏è Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 ‚òïÔ∏è Kei Coffee House (17.38M) 15691 Brookhurst St, Westminster, CA 92683 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Saturday Road Ride - On Orbit & Soda Springs

Let‚Äôs grind up some steep gradients this Saturday. We last sweated this route out in May, which necessitated an extra bottle in our jersey pockets. Conditions should be much more favorable this time, but you‚Äôll want a layer for the summits. We roll over to Saratoga, climb Bohlman the fun way (left on Norton, left on On Orbit, left on Bohlman), descend Montevina, wind around the reservoir to Soda Springs, chug up that to the gate. Then we take a little detour left on Weaver because it‚Äôs so scenic (just make sure to stop at the bottom before the driveway or you‚Äôll make friends with some dogs). Then we head back on the creek trail. Short & steep.

7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes üå• 57f ‚ûú üå§ 68f Flat Pace: 17-19mph Distance: ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation: üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òï Rye Goods (17.9M) 15771 Red Hill Ave Suite 110, Tustin, CA 92780 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Recruitment Ride (A Route)

This Saturday is our annual recruitment ride. Come ride some of our favorite haunts, then join us for gelato on the club at Dolce Spazio. We head out over Shannon to McKean, with a rest stop at Calero park. We then take Bailey up to the feature climb, Metcalf. After regrouping at the top, we‚Äôll descend the backside and loop back around to IBM hill. After that, we wind our way to Kennedy and head back to the shop. There is also alternate route for those would like to skip the Metcalf loop and go directly to IBM hill.

Group Road Ride - Up 9, down Redwood Gulch

This route is the clockwise version of the regular Redwood Gulch route (2nd Sunday of the month as of this posting). This gives us an opportunity to climb highway 9. One notable change is the out/back after the decent of Redwood Gulch on Stevens Canyon Rd, this adds an additional 4 miles to the total. Before the intersection with Mt. Eden we will stop at Cooley Picnic Area on the left for bathrooms and water. After a quick stop we continue around the reservoir and then follow neighborhood roads back to Mike‚Äôs Bikes.

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÅ 58f ‚ûú üå§ 75f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- ‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Columbus Tustin Park 14652 Prospect Ave, Tustin, CA 92780 ‚òïÔ∏è Mameya Coffee Roasters (18.95M) 27931 La Paz Rd E, Laguna Niguel, CA 92677 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

AV-C Ride Oct 26th, 2024 - Crestview via Palomar and Woodridge Climb

Meet: 9:00 AM, Leave: 9:15 AM We will be going north Saturday, and the weather forecast looks favorable. We will get up to Crestview via Palomar. There are many turns up Palomar, so just follow the signs to keep on Palomar. We have a very short regroup at the gate and a longer regroup at Crestview Park. We will follow Crestview and then Ralston to Crystal Springs with a connection to Woodridge. We will then go up Woodridge climb and connect with Black Mountain Rd. We will then head back on Skyline-Canada and the last main regroup will be at the Water Temple. Planned Regroups: Mountain Home and 84 (Woodside) Crestview Park Skyline and Golf Course Dr. Water Temple Backyard Brew Non-Members: Alto Velo welcomes non-members to join us on our rides. However, non-members must have a Waiver on file with the club. Filling out the waiver is only required one time per year. Ride Etiquette https://www.altovelo.org/ride-rules

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on October 26th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, Let's be back on the road and let's enjoy HW9 that has been recently reopened! The plan for this weekend is to do a classic loop: up HW9, down bear creek and up Big Basin way. As always, we will stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Weather forecast looks great and while temperatures will be likely on the high 70s we will probably enjoy lower temperatures while climbing: however, please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops), and do not forget to eat constantly. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

WC2PB9 6:15 AM Roll out ‚òÄÔ∏è 54f ‚ûú ‚òÄÔ∏è 80f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Covina Station 600 N Citrus Ave, Covina, CA 91723 Coffee break for 20 minutes ‚òïÔ∏è Lou, The French On The Block (32.07M) 4007 W Riverside Dr, Burbank, CA 91505 Lunch break for 40 minutes üçΩ The Back Door Bakery & Cafe (69M) 8349 Foothill Blvd, Sunland, CA 91040 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Gravel Ride on October 19th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, The plan for this weekend is to do something different and go for a nice gravel ride: climb El Sereno, and JNT before looping around and come back to LG through the LG Creek trail. As always, we will be stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Please be gentle with me as I am still new on the dirt :-) Weather forecast looks good, but please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops). As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

LGBRC Sunday Ride

Hi team, This Sunday's ride will approach Hicks Rd. from the South. Wheels will roll at 8:35 and take Shannon to Hicks before heading over Camden and taking the maze to New Almaden. We will stop for water and the bathroom at the New Almaden parking lot before climbing Hicks. We will regroup at the top of Hicks where there is also a bathroom at the Hicks and Umunhum intersection. We'll descend Hicks and head back to MBLG via Shannon and Kennedy.

R72UT9 7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÄÔ∏è 57f ‚ûú ‚òÄÔ∏è 72f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òïÔ∏è Eller Bakery (15.30M) 1651 Placentia Ave, Costa Mesa, CA 92627 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on October 12th, 2024

Dear fellow Teammates, The plan for this weekend is to have a long endurance ride and after climbing Hicks, we will head to Uvas before climbing MetCalf. The plan is to keep the peloton together throughout the all ride, but as always we will stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Notice that the route is designed for "escapes" in case anyone may like to leave early. Weather forecast looks good, but please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops). As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÄÔ∏è 83f ‚ûú ‚òÄÔ∏è 90f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- ‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Via Verde Park & Ride 105 Via Verde Dr Rd, San Dimas, CA 91773 ‚òïÔ∏è Iron & Kin Coffee Co (19.51M) 536 W 1st St, Claremont, CA 91711 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Group Road Ride - Up 9, down Redwood Gulch

This route is the clockwise version of the regular Redwood Gulch route (2nd Sunday of the month as of this posting). This gives us an opportunity to climb highway 9. One notable change is the out/back after the decent of Redwood Gulch on Stevens Canyon Rd, this adds an additional 4 miles to the total. Before the intersection with Mt. Eden we will stop at Cooley Picnic Area on the left for bathrooms and water. After a quick stop we continue around the reservoir and then follow neighborhood roads back to Mike‚Äôs Bikes.

9BJ8B4 7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚õÖ 61f ‚ûú ‚òÄÔ∏è 77f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- üÖøÔ∏è Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ‚òïÔ∏è Succulent Coffee Roasters (17.59M) 17196 Pacific Coast Hwy, Huntington Beach, CA 92649 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on September 21st, 2024

Dear fellow teammates, As the weekend is approaching, it is time to plan another epic adventure. The plan for Saturday is to climb Mt. Umunhum not once but twice :-) The route is designed for easy escapes in case you may not want to complete the whole quest or simply decide that climbing Mt. Umunhum once would be enough. The forecast is for a warm day, so please do not forget to bring plenty of water and to hydrate yourself during the ride. Also bring lots of food, and do not forget to fuel yourself constantly. Note that this ride will not be about speed, but it is meant to help build endurance and strength. If you have any questions, please do not hesitate to reach out! See you on Saturday!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Group Road Ride - Big Basin

Heading up 9 and then down to Big Basin, Bathroom/Water in the park at mile 25. After a chance to admire the big trees we head to Boulder Creek (Water/Bathroom at mile 35). After a short break we head to the feature climb of the day, East Zayante Rd., left on Summit, left on Bear Creek, right on Skyline and at mile 61 we stop at Castle Rock (water/bathrooms). After Castle Rock it is mostly downhill to Mikes Bikes. From Boulder Creek (mile 35) to Castle Rock (mile 61) is 26 mostly uphill miles. At mile 45 is Zayante Market, and if the weather is hot I will stop for water

Group Road Ride - Redwood Gulch

Route will head along Winchester Blvd and left onto Dave‚Äôs. We will travel the neighborhoods until we come out on Stevens Canyon Rd. At the intersection with Mt. Eden we will stop at Cooley Picnic Area on the right for bathrooms and water. After a short stop you have the option to (1) go over Mt Eden to Saratoga (2) follow Stevens Canyon Rd to the end and then do Redwood Gulch (for an additional 4 miles), or (3) straight to Redwood Gulch. Due to construction we will CAREFULLY and SLOWLY descend Highway 9, being careful to avoid running into a stopped car at the Sanborn Creek bridge. We will regroup with those who chose Mt Eden in Saratoga and enjoy an easy spin back to Mike‚Äôs Bikes.

DW58JF 7 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ‚òÄÔ∏è 73f ‚ûú ‚òÄÔ∏è 96f Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- ‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Santa Ana Pony Baseball 1999 W 19th St, Santa Ana, CA 92706 üç© Specialized - Costa Mesa (30.27M) 1901 Harbor Blvd, Costa Mesa, CA 92627 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Saturday Road Ride - Henry Coe

This Saturday we dial back the intensity a bit. At 80 miles, it‚Äôs not short, but most of it is flat or rollers getting to and from the feature. Lots of opportunities to save energy with smart pacelining. The feature is Henry Coe, another one of those great climbs that‚Äôs kinda tough to get to from Los Gatos. If we‚Äôre lucky, maybe we‚Äôll get to see some tarantulas crossing the road. Planned rest stops are at Calero on the way out, and at the top of Henry Coe. We can add one on the way back as needed. This ride will be fast paced, but we'll be sure to regroup at key points.

CT7MA9 7:15 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes Distance - ‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è Elevation- ‚≠êÔ∏è üÖøÔ∏è Bill Barber Memorial Park 4 Civic Center Plaza, Irvine, CA 92606 ‚òïÔ∏è High Tide Coffee (21.43M) 27271 La Paz Rd Unit A, Laguna Niguel, CA 92677 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] - Saturday Road Ride on August 31st, 2024 {Century Ride}

Dear fellow Teammates, As the summer is almost at the end, please join us for a century ride along the Santa Cruz Mountains. Since we will have a long day biking, the plan is to keep a steady pace so that to keep the peloton together throughout the all ride, but as always we will stop and regroup at the top of each climb and at the bottom of every descent. Notice that the route is designed for "escapes" in case anyone may like to only do half-century or only part of it. Weather forecast looks good, but please make sure to bring plenty of water (even though we are planning for at least two water stops). As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.
